B. Matcrial Processed

In October, the Scatton was provided by the LIENVOY LP with 135

pages uf daily resumes from all lines, lo pages of resumce from the Cuban

Ines, 17 pages from the Czech lines and 12l pagus from the Soviet lies.

In addition the taped reels from the Soviet and Cauch Iines were turned over

for the transcription of the Russian and Cacch conversatlong. There were

also provided 11 pleces of other miscellandous materlal.

C. Lialson

Because of the urgency of business during the month of Ocruiet, the

COS met with LIERGO and LIELEGANT more frequently, LITENSOR es-

pressed his gratefulness through LIELEGANT on provlling, him with repores:

on the political scene in the Far list countric's that he had visited. On 25

Ocrober, LITENSOR was given the report on the Cuban aluation which was

sent to the Station In DIR 44302, LITENSOR was also shown pholos of the

Soviet missile bases in Cuba, After mecring with high-lovel Mexican efficials,

the Chief of Station reported in MEXI 2397 on their attitudes of the U.S..

quarantine of Cuba and the stopping of further progreds on Soviet missile

bases there.

D. Exploitation of Material

arcempt of Vicente Lombardo Toledano, prominent leftlet Mexican politician.

to make an appolntment witli the Mexican Government In regard to Cuba,

Lombardo Tolcuano was prompted by General Lazaro Cardenas to trito

influence the President. (see MEXI 2402)

ne new LIENVOY LP.

dally resumes, 40 pages of resumes from the Cuban lines and 35 other

C. Exploitation of Material

The following are examples of Information obtained through LIENVOY.

1. In a telephone conversation from San Luis Porosi, Col.

Renato Vega Amador, DFS Chiel, told Capt, de la Barrera of the

Mexico City DFS that "things are happening in San Luis Potost",

and that "something bad would happen" in Monterrey and Mexico

City againsi the Federal Govemnient and that of the State of San

Luis Potost, (MEXI 1600)

2. Joe Nordmann, Secretary of the International Assoclation of

Democratic Lawyera (LADL), spoke with Angelica Arcnal de Alfaro

Siqueiros about his plan to see the President of Mexico to have David

Alfaro Siquelros released from prison. (MEXI 1676)

3. According to employees of the Prensa Latina, employees had

not been paid for some time and the financial situation of the Agency

was "desperate". (MEXI 1670)

10 August 1960

MENORANDUM FOR:

SUBJEC'I:

REFERENCE:

Chick, WH/3

CW Signals on Telephone Tap

HIMMA-14977, 19 May 1960

1. A technical analysis of referoncestap indicates that the

CW Morse signals probably were picked up incidental to the primary

cap and did not actually occur on Line Iz. This is borne out both

from a technical standpoint (signal to noise ratio, oxtraneous CW

signals, etc.) as well as from the contes? of the mossages them.

selves.

The lattor, as will be noted in the altached transcript,

primarily concern arrivals and departures of what appear to be

small maritime voasels. The two radio calls mentioned, 1. o.

"XBRB2" and "XBRP", are listed in tho International Call Sign

Book as follows:

XBRB - Vera Cruz (19-10N, 96-15W)

XBRP - Pichilingue (24- 12N, 110-20 W)

The originating station in this case was Pichilingue.

Hadyszaftstiore is some good reason why a port.

authority on the west coast of Mexico would be sending trailic of

this nature to an east coast port. However, jin, how these

particular signals happened in be picked up on'

Slim Brooks lino

is open to conjecture, It is our guess shat it probably was due

to one of the following reasona:

strong radio frequency signals which possibly are being

rectified by the tap itself.

SEGMET

---

## Page 184

alton:

bo

The equipment used in conjunction with the tap

may be serving as a poor radio receivar, using the telephone

Line as au antenna.

C. The CW signals possibly are being picked up

inductively, le. from another phone line which is in

close proximity to Line 42. This theory seems unlikely,

however, since the transmission of CW signals from one

const to the other via telephone lines would be a slow and

impractical procedure.

3. From tho standpoint uf sechnical interest, mo

scantiate any of the above conjectures.

furnish additional analysis and transcripts should similar signals

be noted in the future.

WILLIANK. HARVEY

Chics, FI Division D

Attachment:
